et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	"And it is necessary for him to grasp the fetus with his right hand, and place the crook of his left elbow between his ribs on his left side, and push gently with his whole hand until he feels the empty space."
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	"And this is the shape of the hook:"
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	"Then insert another hook, or a third if necessary, so that the extraction is even."
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	"And then pull evenly while moving from side to side so that it comes out more easily, and let the hooks be toothed for better grip, as shown here:"
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	"And if any part remains, then the servant should anoint some of his fingers with oil and insert them into that part and pull from the other side."
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	"And if none remains, then place this hook higher up and do likewise until it all comes out completely."
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	"And if one hand comes before the other and he cannot bring it back for extraction,"
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	"then you should wrap a cloth around it until it all comes out."
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	"Then cut the umbilical cord at the navel or elsewhere, and do likewise for the other hand, leaving two feet."
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	"And if the thighs of the child are large and it is difficult to extract it from the womb, or if its head is sharp-pointed,"
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	"then you should place the pointed dilator between your fingers and widen the opening of the head, and extract the point."
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	"or you can use the instrument called 'almidach', whose shape is shown with the other instruments in the chapter that follows this one,"
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	"And do likewise if the child has a large head naturally."
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	"Then pull out the bones with forceps,"
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	"And if the buttocks come out but are stuck in the anus, then cut until the membranes that are at the opening of the perineum come out."
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	"And if it still cannot come out, then cut it into pieces until you can remove it with your hands."
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	"And if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce it until the membranes burst."
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	"And if the child is presenting by the feet, then the extraction will be easy, and the presentation at the mouth of the womb will also be easy."
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	"And if it is stuck in the belly or the perineum, then you must extract it using a cloth wrapped around your hand."
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	"and cut the belly or the perineum until the membranes burst."
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	"And if the other limbs are delivered but the buttocks remain,"
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	"then the servant should insert his hand deeply into the womb and pull until it reaches the mouth of the womb;"
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	"then place one or two hooks there and pull it out."
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	"And if the mouth of the womb is narrowed due to heatstroke that has occurred there, then one must not attempt to intervene,"
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	"but rather apply moist and greasy substances."
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	"And the midwife should use poultices, and also sieve water to make it soft and moistening."
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	"And if the child is lying on its side and you can straighten it, then treat it as we have said for a live child;"
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	"and if one cannot do so, then pull it out in pieces, leaving no part of the afterbirth behind."
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	"And once you have done this, if the midwife encounters heatstroke in the womb,"
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	"and if bleeding occurs, then apply water with astringent properties, and the midwife should administer other remedies."
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	"I saw a woman in whose belly one child had been bitten by another, and the latter had died as a result."
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	"After many days, she developed an infection in her genitals, which swelled until it opened and began to emit a foul odor."
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	"I was summoned to treat her, and after examining her for some time, I could not heal the wound."
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	"I applied a poultice with strong drawing properties, and eventually two bones came out."
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	"I was very astonished at this, since the belly has no bones."
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	"Then I thought that these must be the bones of a dead child."
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	"I cleaned the wound and extracted many more bones until the woman's condition improved;"
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	"and the woman lived for a long time thereafter, but she still had occasional discharge from that area."
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	"I am recording this chapter here only so that when a master encounters such an unusual occurrence, he will know how to provide assistance."
dou ramener la marris a son leu	"to replace the womb in its proper position"
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	"Hereafter comes the form of the forceps, with which books are opened; and there are two turns at the two ends of the two handles."
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	"However, the hooks should be more slender than the restrictor, and made of ivory or boxwood;"
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	"And let the opening of the wood be two fingers wide, with a margin of one finger's width, and let it be one and a half palms long;"
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	"And attached to the two handles of this same wood are two joints which can be fastened securely at either end, each being about half a palm long or slightly more;"
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	"And these two joints are inserted into the mouth of the womb to open it when one turns the two hooks."
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made from ebony or boxwood, resembling forceps.
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and have two holes and two joints, as you see, each a palm in length and two fingers in width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	And when you see to open the womb with all instruments, make the woman sit on one chair, feet dangling and legs apart.
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	Then put the two handles together into the womb, and hold the top of the instrument between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then open your hand on the instrument, just like you did with tweezers evenly, according to how much you see the mouth of the womb opening until the child comes out as it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all mounted and multiplied in their likeness; and when the physician has prepared them, the more hastily the work is done, the higher they are among men for their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not disdain any instrument that you have not prepared, because their necessity cannot be excused.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the secondine is retained at childbirth, it is necessary that you command the sick woman to hold her breath, then make her sneeze with condition, and press your hands against her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she coughs because of this, all the better.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then take one pot, and make one hole in the lid, and put into it herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as calamint, rue, anise, camomile, cassia, and centory.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in the pot with water over the fire; then put one end of a tube into the hole of the pot and the other end into the mouth of the womb.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	And let it steam until the vapor enters the womb; then make her sneeze as we have said before.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the secondine comes out quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if the secondine remains after this treatment and is not completely expelled, command the woman to wet her left hand in oil of sesame or in musk made from almonds, then put it into the birth canal,
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And seek the tendon; and when she finds it, then grasp it gently and stretch it little by little straightly, so that the marrow does not fall out during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But one must move it lightly to the right and left, then pull on it; it will come and align itself.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	"And if the mouth of the wound is too narrow, we have discussed the cure of sneezing, and fumigation with herbs;"
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	"and if it does not benefit from any of what we have said, then be sure that you do not err in the treatment;"
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	"but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the wound, you tie it to the woman's hip, and then perform an enema with oil made from four drugs;"
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	"If it [the wound] becomes inflamed and recurs, and comes to a boil; but nevertheless, when it becomes inflamed there is also a bad odor in the stomach and head, and it harms the patient."
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	"Therefore, it is necessary to perform fumigations with these [ingredients]: none of the ancients have proven fumigation with watercress and dried figs."
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	"The form of the instrument with which one fumes the woman to retain the fetus and the afterbirth is this:"
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	"And it is like a vessel made of glass, and one puts the narrow end into the nature [vagina], and the wide ends over the fire;"
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	"and let the fumigation be done on the coals, until the cloth is completely exhausted, then start another one."
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	"Many children are born whose anus has not been pierced, but was stopped up by a subtle membrane:"
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	"therefore it is the midwife's duty to pierce that membrane with her thumb and not with a sharp point, and to guard against touching it."
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on a linen cloth soaked in wine and oil, then apply the ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	"And if you doubt that it may close up again, then put a tube of lead into the hole and leave it there for several days, and remove it when the child is ready to go to bed."
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	"And sometimes this stoppage comes from a sudden wound or an abscess; therefore one must cut off that sudden growth: if it is cured, then treat it as we have said for the lead tube."
de la fistule dou fondement	of a fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come underneath the anus are nodular and larger than those that come beside the anus or in the space of the two buttocks,"
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	"If there is one fistula or several; and when that nodule is ancient, it opens up, and becomes moist with white pus or subtle bowels,"
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	"and sometimes these fistulas are persistent; and they are recognized by the fact that there is discharge or windiness when the patient evacuates, and sometimes a worm jumps out."
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	"And there are fistulas that pierce up to the bladder and up to half of the penis; and they reach up to the hip joint and up to the knee."
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	"And thus one recognizes a persistent fistula of the anus, and not a persistent one:"
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	"and it is that you put your two index fingers into the anus, and insert a fine needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no tortuosity."
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	"And if it has tortuosity, then insert a thin tube of lead or a horsehair until you feel the tube or the hair with your finger."
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	"and if you do not feel it and nothing comes out through the hole except for pus, wind or a worm, as we have said:"
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	"know that it does not pierce; so hurry to cure it."
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	"And when the fistula is persistent up to the bladder or up to the urinary canal, urine comes out and it cannot be cured by medications."
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	"If it has pierced up to the hip joint, then the tube comes out at that spot;"
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	"if there is no tortuosity and there is inflammation around the pain, then it is that bowels come out constantly, and there is no use for medication or cutting by ointment;"
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	"and in these persistent fistulas there is no other cure except surgery, and the foolishness of those physicians who meddle with them."
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	"In that which is not persistent and is not ancient, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have proven,"
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	"And it is that the patient lies on his belly with his hands under him and raises his legs up to his hips, and inclines his hips towards his belly;"
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	"then insert a brass or lead tube until you know where the tube comes out."
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	"If the patient feels it around the anus, then you must put your two index fingers in there,"
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	"then feel that the tube has pierced it; and if you feel between your finger the sinus or the flesh, then know that it is persistent;"
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	"so do not work on it unless one can cure it."
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	"It is said that one can sometimes cure some of them, but this happens rarely;"
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	"and the help given there consists in heating a fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as it is said before;"
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	"and put it in hot into the fistula until it reaches the anus and do this two or three times until you know that those rotted flesh are burned, which resemble a feather;"
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	"and then cure it with moist tubes smeared with butter until that flesh comes out, and then cure it with an ointment that heals the skin and binds the wound."
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	"If it is thus cured, it is well. But if it cannot be cured otherwise;"
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	"and if the tube enters but does not reach your finger that is in the anus and there is a thick covering of flesh or sinus between your two fingers and the tube, and you see the fistula through this covering;"
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	"then cut off the beginning of the fistula and push the tube in again and then use the cautery until it reaches the end of the tube;"
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	"and the tube will be delivered and fall out; then remove that rotted flesh which resembles a feather, and nothing will remain."
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	"And if the pus comes between you and your work, then cauterize it with fire or an acrid medication."
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	"For the cautery of fire combines two good things: namely, the burning of that rotted flesh and the stopping of bleeding and the drying of humidity;"
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	"then cure it with moist tubes smeared with butter or crushed herbs until the spot becomes empty and burned flesh comes out in the bowels;"
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	"then cure the wound with healing ointments that bind and harden the skin, which are dry medications."
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	"For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return."
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	"And if a fistula comes out deeply from the anus and is far from the body, put your two fingers into the anus and inquire after it."
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	"If you feel the tube and between your two fingers there is a cloth or sinus or flesh where it is about to pierce, then there is nothing else but to go through with faith and hope by administering one of these three methods:"
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	"either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it off completely, or if you push it in you put tubes in and cure it as before."
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	"and do not go too deeply that you cut the tissue that holds the anus in place, and cause involuntary evacuations;"
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then the treatment, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perhaps it will heal if you remove that covering and clean the area around its base with water or some other pointed tool;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	"Then cleanse as much of the wound's matter as you are able."
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	"And then study how to restore the wound and keep the fistula away from the fundament: it will be easier for the patient."
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	"And some times fistulas occur in this manner: when you put your finger into the fistula and it is situated at the side of the fundament near the skin above,"
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	"If you take a needle pierced at its head like this:"
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	"And wrap one thread twice around it, and push the needle entirely into the fistula until it reaches the end."
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	"If the fistula is situated within the margin of the fundament internally, then pull out the thread from that hole so that you may place your finger on the fundament;"
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	"and tie the end of the thread and bring both ends together, tying them to each other tightly, leaving it for one or two days;"
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	"And tighten it sometimes until the threads cut through those tissues that are between them and dry up;"
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	"Then treat the wound until it is healed and healthy."
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	"But if the fistula does not open up on its own, then make an incision in any way that you are able to, if it is not too deeply embedded."
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"For one should not attempt to cut something that is too deeply embedded and then treat it as we have said, until it is healed."
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	"The shape of the spatula used for opening a fistula should be sharp and pointed at one end and cutting:"
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	"And on the other end it should not be sharp, so that you do not cut what you should not."
des emorroydes	"hemorrhoids"
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	"Hemorrhoids occur in two ways: either they are internal within the fundament, like grains of resin, and there can be both small and large ones; sometimes they bleed externally;"
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	"and there can be one or several of them that are prolapsed from the fundament and at the head of the fundament; but those that are prolapsed have little moisture;"
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	"And externally they appear as a bit of clear watery fluid or a bit of blood, and they have the color of flesh;"
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	"The treatment for those who have hemorrhoids internally within the fundament is to command the patient to strain while attempting to defecate in a privy until the fundament prolapses and the veins appear;"
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	"then quickly seize it with forceps or hold it with your thumb and forefinger, then cut it at its base;"
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	"And if the fingers cannot hold them due to their moisture, then grasp them with a cloth or cotton or a piece of linen;"
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	"and pull them out with your two hands, then cut them and apply some warm powders instead of cauterization;"
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	"or cauterize them as is described in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed."
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	"And if the fundament cannot prolapse, then administer to the patient a strong and sharp enema to wash out what is inside the fundament so that it can protrude openly;"
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	"once the patient has relieved themselves, if the veins are protruding from the fundament, then the treatment is simple;"
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	"And this involves grasping them with your thumb and forefinger or with forceps, then cutting them; afterwards treat them as we have said until they are healed, so that the patient fears the incision by iron no more."
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	"You should prepare the stitch as follows: take one twisted thread and insert it into a needle; then pull the thread up from above and pierce the needle through from below, then turn both ends of the thread under the needle:"
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	"And make it tight; then tie the thread in a knot and remove the needle, and do this for all of them except one that you leave to drain any excess blood;"
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	"then place one moist cloth soaked in rose oil or wax on the fundament and tell the patient to lie down;"
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And then wait until they defecate; once they have done so, treat them with ointments and other remedies until they are healed."
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	"Regarding the drying of fistulas in the fundament:"
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	"Many times there is drying out of fistulas in the intestines, either due to natural constriction or when the illness is old and medicinal treatments are ineffective;"
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	"You should use the tip of a spatula or your fingernail to scrape off the moist outer layer without causing bleeding;"
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	"then treat it until it is healed as it ought to be;"
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	"And if it cannot heal, then begin scraping again more forcefully than before, until it heals completely and is completely scraped;"
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	"then treat it until it is healed."
dou fremit	"Regarding tremors:"
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	"A tremor is a small, sudden movement that occurs within the body and spreads deeply;"
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	"And sometimes it strikes one with coldness, and it feels like death from trembling; it can affect the entire body, but more often affects the hands than any other part;"
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	"The treatment involves taking a goose quill or a strong crow feather and placing it on the tremor until the circle of its tip encompasses the tremor entirely;"
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	"then twist your hand around the entire quill until you cut all around the tremor and drive it deep into its roots;"
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	"And if you see fit to do so, use a feather made of brass or iron in this same manner, making sure it is thin underneath and pointed above;"
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	"Do not pierce too deeply to avoid causing pain and injury; if you wish, cauterize the tremor as is described earlier in the chapter on cautery."
de la forme dou clistere	"Regarding the form of an enema:"
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	"Sometimes an enema is made of silver or brass, or molten bronze or moistened iron; and sometimes these instruments are small or large according to their intended purpose;"
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	"Therefore, those that should be used for treating children and the weak and infirm are small;"
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	"The shape of a small or large enema is as follows, depending on how full the belly is:"
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	"And it should have one opening at the tip and two openings on one side and one on the other;"
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	"and the belly itself is made from an animal bladder or parchment and pierced with many small holes all around;"
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	"and each hole has a small disk of lead placed over it; then insert through these holes one strong thread made of twisted hair, doubled or however many times around you wish, and sew the belly closed like a purse;"
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	"And when the medicinal substance is inside, tie it to the instrument in front with a strong thread and administer the enema; this is called the circular form;"
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	"And let the medicinal substance be neither too hot nor too cold; grease the tip of the enema with oil or axle-grease from a cart-wheel or something similar and insert it gently;"
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	"then the administrator presses with both hands together until all of it has been inserted; then remove the enema and raise the patient's legs toward the wall;"
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	"and if any medicinal substance remains inside, squeeze it out as much as possible; and if he sleeps all night without getting up, it will be more beneficial."
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if you perform a clyster for an illness of diarrhea of the bowels, and the doctor rushes to remove it, then reapply it until it is clean."
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	"And if hemorrhoids are on the fundament or an ulcer, then the clyster should be as subtle as for a [child of] one year old;"
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	"and this is the form of the subtle clyster onto which the skin is stretched:"
des plaies	"of wounds"
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	"We have already spoken in the division about the treatment of wounds; now we will tell you about treatments for hands and medicines according to their completion."
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	"I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made from, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and from what they are made."
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	"The things by which wounds are made are by cutting of stone, and cutting of sword and knife, or of spear or club or staff, or of similar things;"
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	"or are made according to the places on the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or on the head, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members;"
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	"And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory [of their treatment] will come in its chapter."
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	"I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, one should take care if it was made by cutting of stone or similar things, and if the skin is completely torn and the wound is large,"
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	"and immediately remove the hot aposteme: if it comes out little blood from the wound, then perform a cautery with the cautery iron itself, and let the cautery be on the opposite side of the wounded part;"
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	"and avoid excessive drinking of wine and heavy foods."
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	"And if it does not want to cauterize, then let his food be softened, and he should not drink wine nor eat meat;"
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	"and place on the wound, if hot apostemes come out, cotton moistened in rose oil only, or in astringent wine;"
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	"And if there is no hot aposteme, then place on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood and has not been moved by air, powder which I will tell you about a little later;"
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"and if the air has moved it, then place some ointments on it until it is healed."
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	"And if the wound is large like that of a sword cut or similar ones, and its lips cannot come together by themselves, then bring them together by stitching, as I will tell you about stomach wounds regarding stitching."
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	"If the wound is open to the bone and hangs down and holds only by a little, then cut it off. Then treat the wound with medicines, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,"
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	"and command the sick person to eat heavy foods such as testicles and cooked wheat, also like poultry and similar things."
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	"And if you find putrefaction in the skin but not on the bone, then cut off all the rotting flesh and cast it away, and then treat [the wound]."
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	"And if there is an artery or vein in the wound that bleeds without stopping and cannot be stopped by medications, then find the artery. And if you find it severed, then tie it with a thread;"
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	"and if this does not help, then cauterize it."
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	"And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is easy: you should put in this powder which seals before air moves it."
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	"The manner of preparing the powder is as follows: take incense one part, dragon's blood two parts, and quicklime three parts, and grind it subtly,"
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	"and fill the wound with it, and press strongly until it is well absorbed and joins with all its blood;"
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	"and then bind it well and let it rest without undoing it unless it becomes swollen; for one does not remove the medication until it is healed."
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	"And sometimes this [treatment] is done with quicklime alone when one does not have incense nor dragon's blood, provided that air has not moved the wound."
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	"And if air has moved the wound, especially in summer, then one should not put this powder [on it] at all;"
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	"but place some digested ointments or poultices made of barley flour and water and honey on it until it weeps;"
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	"then treat it with other treatments until it is healed."
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	"And if a bone fracture comes with the wound and it is small, then extract it with delicate forceps;"
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	"and I will tell you about fractures of the head later on."
de la plaie dou col	"About wounds to the neck:"
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	"If a wound comes on the neck and it is simple, then there is no difference between it and one on the head, except that if the nerves of the neck or an artery are cut."
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	"If it is a nerve, then there is no other remedy than to leave it alone and not put anything constricting on it, because it harms the nerves and makes them withdraw;"
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	"and do not put anything cold on the wound, because the substance of nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member;"
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	"but let the medication be warm, such as hot water washed in sweet water and mixed with rose oil, and cooked water also washed in sweet water;"
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	"and other similar things according to this manner, and moist ointments."
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if the wound is large, then stitch it up and bind it with bandages, and treat it until it is healed."
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	"And if the wounds are deep and filled with pus, then prick them lower down;"
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	"and if an artery is cut and bleeding continues to flow from it, then relieve the pressure on it, tie it off, and cauterize it if necessary;"
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	"and if the spine of the neck or the heart is cut but the vessels through which the flesh goes are preserved,"
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	"then stitch up the heart to the spine of the neck and do not touch the throat but put it back according to its natural shape;"
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	"and then press it forward gently, leave it for a few days, and then treat it with drying ointments until it is healed."
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	"And if the wound has made an impression on the bone, then search for it;"
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	"and if there are pieces of bone, then remove them all if you can, and those that you cannot have removed, leave them until the wound rots;"
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	"and relieve the pressure on it and clean out the discharge;"
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	"And if the wound is fresh, then sprinkle on the powder that I have mentioned."
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	"And if there are bones and fistulas in the wound, then treat it as I said in its chapter."
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	"About wounds from lances or knives:"
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	"If it is a blow from a lance or a knife and the wound is deep, then look to see if wind sounds come from the wound when the sick person breathes: know then that the wound is mortal;"
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	"and if it is not deep but fresh with all its blood, then do not put on the powder at first nor tie it up so that the blood does not drain too deeply;"
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	"and return to the heart, and kill the patient;"
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	"But apply attractive ointment, and wrap it twice a day."
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	"And if you do not have ointment, then put old cotton in the wound to suck out the moisture."
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	"And make the patient lie on the wound for 3 days, or 4 days, or more."
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	"If there is no spasm, nor trembling of the heart, nor pulling of the sinews;"
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	"And when you see that the bones are well positioned, then know that the wound is healed."
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	"Then treat it with poultices and other remedies until he is healed;"
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	"And if it cannot heal nor close up, then know that there is a fistula, and treat it accordingly."
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	"And if the wound is from an incision made by a sword or knife, and it is simple, or worse on the back side, treat it as those on the front are treated;"
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	"If it is large, suture it; and if it is small, use powder on it. And if it is close to the bone, and has cut off pieces, then scrape the wound clean, and treat the edges separately if they are separated;"
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	"And if they are not separated, let the wound heal by itself, for it will expel the foreign bodies."
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	"And for wounds on other members, the judgment is as we have said before."
dou derrompement dou ventre	"On rupture of the abdomen:"
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	"A rupture of the abdomen can be large, medium, or small;"
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	"From a large wound sometimes the intestines or the mesentery protrude, causing an obstruction;"
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	"And suturing is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one,"
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because when one resets them roughly, the intestines slip back in;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell immediately upon feeling the coldness and thus slip back in roughly
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and because it is beneficial to move the membrane wound, so that one can reset the intestines into their place without moving the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that a hole in the abdomen can occur in four ways
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common suture lines occur along the abdominal wall
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and two other sutures proper to other wounds are common to those wounds
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	but nonetheless they are more proper with the abdominal suture, and I will describe each one and explain it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small and none of the intestines are protruding
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and the matter is simply one of resetting, it occurs in two ways
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen from the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat them in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	soak a sponge or one soft cloth in hot water alone
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or boil in hot water with cinnamon and cumin
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and warm the intestines until the swelling is gone;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And sometimes this constraining wine is made, and it is said to be useful for releasing wind.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	When you see the swelling starting to disappear, moisten the intestine with water or oil, and let it cook until it is soft
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for by this means the entrance of the intestine is opened somewhat;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	"And if it cannot enter, then make a small cut in the wound with the instrument used to remove hemorrhoids;"
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	"The first treatment is to move the bone that sticks out,"
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	"which we should not cut unless there is great necessity;"
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	"And this is the instrument for splitting:"
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	"If it cuts within the curve but not outside, see here its shape:"
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	"And when the wound is widened and the intestines protrude"
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	"if you replace them according to their natural form in their proper place,"
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	"if you have the ability to do so, for it is necessary."
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	"If the wound is wide and it is located below the belly,"
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	If you must have the patient lie on his back.
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	And put his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the lower abdomen
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	then raise the head and breast higher than the lower parts.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	And also, if the hernia of the belly is in one of the two sides
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	then make sure that the injured part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus it should be arranged in cases of large and medium-sized hernias.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	In small hernias, do what you are familiar with.
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have one gentle assistant who carefully pulls out all the hernia with his hand
et assemble les levres;	and bring together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	And this is the common method of suturing
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	It is that you take one needle or more, according to the quantity of the width of the wound
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave at the beginning of the wound two spans' worth of space and there insert a needle with one good strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce both heads of the skin with both heads of the sinew
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is underneath the skin inside, until you have pierced it through that part
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and bring together both heads of the sinew with four stitches together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	Then tie a double thread around the needle on both sides
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then bring together both heads of the wound evenly;
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	And then leave two spans' worth of space and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	Then tie off the thread in the same way that you did with the first needle
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue to do this until you have used enough needles
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is closed;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And let the needles be medium-sized, between thin and thick ones;
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	For fine needles pierce all the flesh, and those that are too large cannot go in very well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Therefore they should be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	And do not push the needles too deep into the flesh and skin
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	lest they pierce and open the wound before it is closed;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	Then cut off the heads of the needles so that they do not hurt the sick person while sleeping
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	And put tents or bandages at the heads of the needles to keep them in place
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them there until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	And this method of suturing with needles is more appropriate for small wounds
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	For it suffices to use one or two needles there
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitching is common
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And it is that you bring together both heads of the skin and both heads of the sinew with one needle with a medium-strength thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced all these four heads together
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	Then turn the needle back on itself at the part where you began, in the manner that one sews cloth;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	And leave a space between each stitch equal to the width of two fingers;
ceste costure sevent li home,	This stitching serves well
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	I sewed a wound that a man had in his belly
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	that was cut with a knife
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	And the wound was more than a palm's width long
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and there were two palms' worth of intestines sticking out of it
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	And the wound was in his belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	"I then replaced the intestine after he had been unconscious for 24 hours."
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	"The wound was healed for fifteen days, I dressed it, and it became healthy."
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	"And the physicians had judged him to die, but this was a miracle."
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	"and I did not treat it with ointment because I was in one place where none were found nor any medicine."
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	"And place old cotton twice daily above the wound, washing it with honey water until it is clean."
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	"I will tell you two proper methods of suturing:"
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle and insert it from the outer part to the inner one;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When it has pierced the heart from right to left, then place the tip of the siphon or costal tube where you have inserted the needle.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	Then pierce it through another part of the side until it reaches that one.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	"And the meaning of this stitch is that you should sew it as skinner's do skins,"
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	"and leave once the thread on one side and take it up again on the other until the seam is complete."
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second manner of sewing, which Galen discusses specifically
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is such that certain individuals join the two parts together naturally
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one end of the sinew to the other end in this manner
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stick a needle near the end of the membrane and pierce it just once
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave the two ends of the sinew;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle around and pierce it from the outside part to the inside part
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	the two ends of the sinew.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce both from the outside part to the inside part with two other needles placed on either side of it;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the second manner of sewing, and the most common.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen called this technique "the closed method," some testify to it
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	that one should sew the abdomen with two needles, each having thread;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and place one needle on this side and the other on that side, in the manner of those who sew hides;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the intestine is inside the abdomen
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the stitching is closer together than other parts of the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The assessment of this wound is similar to that of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is said that when you find the wound fresh with all its blood before the art has moved it
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	then remove the intestine and the stitching, then apply powdered resin around the flesh;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the art has moved it, then apply some ointment that is at hand, until the wound closes;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	And draw the threads, and make the bandages strong, and the poultice.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then heal the wound as you would any other, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	"And if you don’t have any medicine, then immediately apply cotton wool when it begins to discharge pus."
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	"And move it twice a day until it is clean."
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	Because you have no need for other medicine in many cases when wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	And if you doubt that the wound does not communicate with main joints,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	"If you must wet light linen with warm olive oil, or rose oil,"
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	"And wrap it around the angles and under the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	"If there is pain or putrefaction in his bowels, and this happens many times,"
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	"if black wine enemas help, especially if the putrefaction reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	"And know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small one."
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	"The 'small' intestine cannot be healed when it is injured,"
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	"and this is due to the narrowness of its vessels and the delicacy of all the body's parts, as well as its proximity to nerves."
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	"And if the spleen comes out from the wound, put it back in just like the intestine, while it is still fresh;"
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	"and if it's old and has turned towards worms or blackness, then tie the vessel that is black so that no more blood flows."
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	for there are veins and arteries there.
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then cut what is between the liver
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	"And place the two kidneys hanging down from below the wound until they reach the edge to facilitate the spleen's removal and close the wound."
de la routure dou boueil	of the bowel's rupture
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestine is intact and the wound is small,"
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	"some people can recover from it,"
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	for I saw a man who was pierced in the belly with a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	And the wound was on the right side of the stomach
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became inflamed and turned into a fistula; both pus and wind were excreted through it
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated him according to what I could, and did not cease until he was healed; the place was solid.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw that it had healed, I doubted whether the patient might have some illness in his belly
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no evil, but he remained in better condition, eating and drinking
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And certain surgeons said that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it should be bound in this manner
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	Take large leaves of cabbage and then gather together the edges of the wound
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the leaf has opened its mouth, place it on both lips
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it draws out its mouth from above;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	And then he cuts off the head, which remains thus so that it cannot untie itself.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	Then he puts another suture in this manner as before until the wound is completely closed.
et cout la plaie.	And sew up the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	Those heads will become absorbed into the intestines and cause no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	"And one may tie the intestine with a fine thread cut from an animal's intestine,"
en teil maniere:	"in this manner:"
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	"Take the head of this intestinal thread that is very skinned,"
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	And then tie at the head of this thread one thread of fine twisted linen
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then insert the thread into the needle and sew up the intestines, and reset the dislocation in the incision;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	"And this method of stitching wounds is not performed except according to the way of trust and hope;"
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	"However, if the wound is large and wide, especially when it affects one of the major internal organs, then there is no hope except for subtlety."
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	"of fistula wherever it may be"
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	"Know you that every wound or abscess, when it grows wide, is universally called 'fistula'.
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And similarly when it is hollowed out and opens inward.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	"A fistula is truly a broken vein with hard, white swelling that causes no pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	"and it is also crooked like the feather of a bird;"
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	"And sometimes thin with clear bow, and other times thick;"
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	"Sometimes small, and other times large;"
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	"And I spoke of it in the section on wounds that any wound which is not healed and has no flesh,"
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	"is only healed through one of the eight causes:"
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	"That is to say, by the smallness of the blood or flesh;"
ou por sa malice;	"or for its wickedness;"
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	"or because there is hard flesh inside and on the lips that does not allow flesh to grow;"
ou il i a trop de bowe;	"or if there is too much bow;"
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	"or if the wound is putrid, and the matter is of poor quality;"
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	"or if the medicine is not good in the healing;"
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	"or because corruption is a type of pestilence;"
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	"or due to the property in the region being slow in digestion, and delayed healing, and naturally weak;"
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	"or if there are veins or bones:"
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	"I have already shown all these causes, signs, and remedies of medicine in the section."
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	"Now I must tell you about the treatment for fistula that is performed by handiwork."
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	"Know that fistula occurs in all parts of the body;"
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	"for there are fistulas that come from large veins, arteries, and nerves,"
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	"or the spleen, intestines, bladder, or any of the ribs,"
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	"or the spine of the back, or any joint of the hands or feet;"
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	"And sometimes it comes from the property of the main member and similar places."
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	"And all fistules that are of this kind are difficult to heal, except by labor and ignorance;"
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	"But if there is any fistula which does not come from the places I have said, you can be confident of its treatment,"
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	"And if you see it and recognize it, take an awl or iron rod, if the fistula is straight, then bore it;"
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	"If the fistula is crooked, search for it with a fine lead awl,"
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	"for lead bends more easily around the crookedness;"
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	"And if the fistula has multiple openings and you cannot find it well with awls,"
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	"then rinse it through one of the openings;"
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	"for the moisture will then flow from one opening to another and cleanse it."
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	"Then probe it strongly with your finger, so that you may know if there is bone or nerve, and how deep it goes;"
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	"And ask the patient carefully about the pain they feel when you press with your hand, and where they feel it;"
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	"and once you truly know where it is, and if it is far from a joint, nerve, artery or vein,"
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	"then cut according to what I have told you;"
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	"And remove the defect and rotted tissue inside;"
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	"Then heal it until it is healed,"
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	"If the fistula goes very deep in a straight direction, you must cut deeply, as far as you can;"
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	"Then place moistened awls medicated with hot water into the fistula until they reach its head;"
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	"until the medication corrodes all the surplus matter left at the bottom."
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	"And then place clean, healthy bandages on it until it is healed;"
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	"If it does not heal with this method, then cauterize it as we have said;"
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	"And if the bone is rotted by the fistula, cut it out."
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	"If vein or nerve does not trouble you in the main members, as we have said;"
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	"And if bone is exposed and there is corruption and blackness, scrape it until all corruption is removed;"
